    %up to 6 compound meanings like '    \item [hiragana] [translation]'

\item あいとう\\*

\item あわれ\\*

\item あいしゅう\\*

\item きどあいらく\\*

\item あいかん\\*

\end{enumerate}%

}%

\begin{flashcard}{
\setlength{\heightlimit}{0.87\cardinnerheight}%

  \parbox{0.4\cardinnerwidth}{%

    \fontsize{80}{80}\selectfont 抑 \\[4pt]
    \fontsize{12}{14}\selectfont 扌 \\[2pt]
  }%
  \setbox0=\hbox{%
  \parbox{0.4\cardinnerwidth}{%
    \fontsize{10}{11}\selectfont
    %up to 6 compounds like '      \item ...'
    \begin{enumerate}[leftmargin=20pt,itemsep=1pt,parsep=2pt,topsep=2pt,partopsep=2pt,font=\normalfont\normalsize]
\item 抑える
\item 抑制
